Average lead time is 10–21 days depending on quantity and destination. For large container orders, please allow additional time for production and logistics coordination.
What is your minimum order quantity (MOQ)?
Our MOQ varies by product type. For container loads, we typically require a minimum of 20 tons. For mixed containers, we can accommodate smaller quantities. Contact us for specific requirements.
What payment terms do you accept?
We accept T/T (wire transfer), L/C (letter of credit), and other standard international payment methods. Terms are typically 30% deposit with balance before shipment, though we can discuss alternatives for established customers.
Do you provide samples?
Yes, we can provide product samples for quality evaluation. Sample costs and shipping are charged separately but can be credited against your first commercial order.
What Incoterms do you support?
We support all standard Incoterms including FOB, CFR, and CIF. We can also arrange door-to-door delivery for certain destinations. Let us know your preferred terms when requesting a quote.
What is the ash content and burn time?
Our premium charcoal has less than 3% ash content and provides 3-5 hours of consistent heat depending on the product type. Each product comes with detailed specifications and certificates of analysis.
